prison astert grace dred nat either thou shalt die thou ne shalt nat louen emelye thou wilt thou shalt astert arcite full dispitous hert hym knewe tale herd fers lion pulled sweard saied god sitteth aboue ne wer thou art sicke wod loue eke thou weapen hast place thou shouldest neuer groue pace thou ne shouldest dien mine honde defie suertie bonde thou saist haue made thee foole thinke wel loue free loue maugre thy might asmoch thou art knight wilnest daren battaile haue mi truth morrow fail without wittyng wight founden knight bringen harneis right inough thee chese best leaue worst meate
